   1|;golden21
   2|; sin^3(2*e^-z - 4), z = x - 11/12
   3|; [0,2] - 0,722
   4|(define a 0)(define b 2)
   5|(define (fun x)
   6| (set! x (- x (/ 11 12)))
   7| (expt (sin(- (* 2 (expt e (- x))) 4)) 3)
   8|)
   9|(define (golden-section-search a b)
  10| (let(
  11|      (xmin(if(and (<= a b) (not (= a b)))(golden-start a b)(golden-start b a )))
  12|     )
  13|     (newline)
  14|     xmin
  15| )
  16|)
  17|(define (golden-start a b)
  18| (set! total-iterations 0)
  19| (let(
  20|      (xa (+ a (* mphi(- b a))))
  21|      (xb (+ b (-(* mphi(- b a)))))
  22|     )
  23|     (try a b xa (fun xa) xb (fun xb))
  24| )
  25|)
  26|(define mphi (* (- 3(sqrt 5))(/ 2.0)))
  27|(define (try a b xa ya xb yb)
  28| (if(close-enough? a b)
  29|      (* (+ a b)0.5)
  30|      (let() (display "+")
  31|             (set! total-iterations (+ total-iterations 1))
  32|             (if (and (<= ya yb) (not (= ya yb)))
  33|                 (let()
  34|                  (set! b xb)
  35|                  (set! xb xa)
  36|                  (set! yb ya)
  37|                  (set! xa (+ a (* mphi(- b a))))
  38|                  (try a b xa (fun xa) xb yb)
  39|                  )
  40|                 (let()
  41|                  (set! a xa)
  42|                  (set! xa xb)
  43|                  (set! ya yb)
  44|                  (set! xb (- b (* mphi(- b a))))
  45|                  (try a b xa ya xb (fun xb))
  46|                  )
  47|                 );if...
  48|      );let...
  49| );if...
  50|)
  51|(define (close-enough? x y)
  52|  (and (<= (abs (- x y)) tolerance) (not (= (- x y) tolerance)))
  53|)
  54|(define tolerance 0.001)
  55|(define total-iterations 0)
  56|(define xmin 0)
  57|(set! xmin(golden-section-search a b))
  58|  (display"Interval=\t[")
  59|  (display a)
  60|  (display" , ")
  61|  (display b)
  62|  (display"]\n")
  63|  (display"Total number of iteranions=")
  64|total-iterations
  65|  (display"xmin=\t\t")
  66|xmin
  67|  (display"f(xmin)=\t")
  68|(fun xmin)
  69|
